=== sources/olden-era.com/text/en/heroes.txt ===
Heroes

At the moment, it is known that Heroes of Might and Magic: Olden Era will feature six factions during the Closed Beta Test. However, the final version of the game and the complete set of unique mechanics for each faction are still subject to change.

Heroes are the heart of the entire game in Heroes of Might and Magic: Olden Era. They lead the army, strengthen it with their skills, gather resources, and ultimately decide who wins. Each hero starts with their own initial army (the count may vary slightly), a unique specialization, fixed starting stats, and a faction class.

Detailed stats, starting troops, and specializations for each hero — check the right menu. Just select the hero you need and explore.

Hero Stats — What They Do

The four main stats grow with levels and directly affect the army:

attack— increases damage of all troops. The higher it is, the harder they hit.

defence— reduces damage taken. The higher it is, the less you get hit in the face.

spell power— enhances spell power (damage, healing, duration).

intelligence— increases mana pool.

Starting values depend on the class. For example, all Warlock (Dungeon mages) start with:

attack0  |defence2  |spell power2  |intelligence3

Stat growth probabilities on levels 1–12 for Warlock (example of a mage):

attack15%  |defence20%  |spell power30%  |intelligence35%

After level 12 — equal 25% chance for each stat.

How to Pump Stats Fast and Hard

Besides levels, there are tons of other ways:

Artifacts — the most powerful and flexible method. Swap gear between heroes — a weak level 1 hero can become a level 12+ monster thanks to good artifacts.

Permanent bonuses from map objects: [], [], [], [], [], [], []and others.

Faction Laws — each faction has its own useful boosts ( [see here]).

 []— chance to get +2/+3/+4 to all stats at once.

Leveling and Experience

Heroes start at level 1. Experience comes from battle victories — the sum of EXP from all killed creatures. Example: killed 10 creatures with 100 EXP each → +1000 experience.

Experience Requirements

1 → 2 and 2 → 3 — 1000 EXP each

3 → 4 — 1200 EXP

After level 20 — around ~20,000 EXP per level

Quick ways to gain experience:

 []— +1000 EXP

 []— immediately +1 level

 []— sacrifice units or artifacts

 []— 6,000–10,000 EXP (once per game)

How to level up a hero as quickly as possible

Useful if you want to unlock powerful subskills and faction abilities early.

 [Expert Insight]— +40% to experience (+10% with theEnlightenment:EnlightenmentThe hero gains an additional +10% XP.subskill)

Hero specializations: [Ister:], [Nihil:]

 [Expert Logistics]— +20%; with [Expert Daylight Magic]→Speed of Light:Speed of Light+10 Movement points. This bonus is doubled if the hero knows “Logistics.”— +20 static points

Objects: [](+20% for a week), [](+40 points/day upon visit)

Laws: Dungeon —5Jadame MapsYour heroes gain 10 Movement points.

Artifacts: [Fallen Angel Wings], [Backpack], [Boots of Travel], [Seven‑League Boots]

Neutral Spells:Second Wind,Shadowflight,Gate of Light,Dimension Door

Feeling dizzy from this whole map?

Don’t worry — just remember a simple rule: native troops = no penalties, roads = fast, any swamp = only withGate of Lightor flying. Transferring armies and chaining cities is an advanced tactic; at the beginning, you can play without it.

Don’t worry if you can’t navigate perfectly the first time — that’s okay. Experience will come, and enjoying the game is more important than any timers or “optimal” routes. Good luck on the map!

Available Subclasses

Broodmother

Doubles the base stats of summoned Fire Larvae.

WightAmnesiac - Wights growth in your cities increases by 2. Under his command, Wights gain 1 Speed, 1 Initiative, and 20% HP. Their Attack and Defence increase by 1 for every 3 hero levels, and enemy Wights lose an equal amount of Attack and Defence.

Specialty:MinotaursMinotaursBalthazar's Lair - Minotaurs growth in your cities increases by 1. Under his command, Minotaurs gain 1 Speed, 1 Initiative, and 20% HP. Their Attack and Defence increase by 1 for every 3 hero levels, and enemy Minotaurs lose an equal amount of Attack and Defence.

MinotaursBalthazar's Lair - Minotaurs growth in your cities increases by 1. Under his command, Minotaurs gain 1 Speed, 1 Initiative, and 20% HP. Their Attack and Defence increase by 1 for every 3 hero levels, and enemy Minotaurs lose an equal amount of Attack and Defence.

Specialty:ConcubiConcubiLeash of Chains - Concubi growth in your cities increases by 1. Under his command, Concubi gain 1 Speed, 1 Initiative, and 20% HP. Their Attack and Defence increase by 1 for every 3 hero levels, and enemy Concubi lose an equal amount of Attack and Defence.

ConcubiLeash of Chains - Concubi growth in your cities increases by 1. Under his command, Concubi gain 1 Speed, 1 Initiative, and 20% HP. Their Attack and Defence increase by 1 for every 3 hero levels, and enemy Concubi lose an equal amount of Attack and Defence.

Specialty:Healing WaterHealing WaterCompassionate Healer - Starts with the “Masterful Healing Water” spell. This version of the spell dispels all negative effects from friendly creatures. While casting this spell, effective Spell Power is increased by 1 for every 3 hero levels.

Healing WaterCompassionate Healer - Starts with the “Masterful Healing Water” spell. This version of the spell dispels all negative effects from friendly creatures. While casting this spell, effective Spell Power is increased by 1 for every 3 hero levels.

Fraction:Temple

Class:Cleric

Specialty:LightweaversLightweaversWeaving the Light - Lightweavers growth in your cities increases by 1. Under her command, Lightweavers gain 1 Speed, 1 Initiative, and 20% HP. Their Attack and Defence increase by 1 for every 3 hero levels, and enemy Lightweavers lose an equal amount of Attack and Defence.

LightweaversWeaving the Light - Lightweavers growth in your cities increases by 1. Under her command, Lightweavers gain 1 Speed, 1 Initiative, and 20% HP. Their Attack and Defence increase by 1 for every 3 hero levels, and enemy Lightweavers lose an equal amount of Attack and Defence.
